Important Proposals from the Huai River Guidance Conference 49

Wang Qingmu's Opinion on Guiding the Huai River into the Sea

During the plenary session of the Huai River Guidance Committee on the 30th, the proposals discussed included Xu Shiying's proposal to guide farmers in developing irrigation projects and negotiations regarding the Italian Boxer Indemnity funds. The most important and fundamental was the plan to guide the Huai River into the sea. Wang Qingmu's original proposal for guiding the Huai River into the sea is recorded below:

It has been over seventy years since the Yellow River changed its course to the north, causing the old course of the Huai River to become silted up. During this period, there have been many proposals to guide the Huai River, and preparations have been made for a long time. Although the goal of actual construction has not been achieved, the guiding principle has always been to release the water into the sea and lower the flood level. Now, the central government is actively proceeding with the Huai River guidance project and has organized a committee in which I, Qingmu, am honored to participate. Having grown up on the coast and being concerned about the benefits and problems of the Jiangsu and Anhui regions, I have some knowledge of the situation. I dare to present a summary of my views. The Huai River flows eastward from Tongbai in Henan for seven hundred *li* to Sanhejian on the border of Henan and Anhui. The mountains and dikes on both banks have always been considered complete and solid. The riverbed slopes steeply, and even if there is accumulated water, it is easily discharged, so there is no significant flooding. From Sanhejian to Bengbu, a distance of four hundred *li*, rivers such as the Ruo, Run, Wo, Qian, Fei, and Ying all flow into the Huai. The length and volume of these rivers are several times greater than that of the Huai River itself, not to mention the countless other tributaries. When there is a lot of water and the slope is gentle, there is no escape from major floods in the autumn. Bengbu is located at the border between Jiangsu and Anhui near Laozi Mountain, a distance of over three hundred *li*. In addition to the tributaries, there are also large rivers such as the Sui, Hui, Tong, Tuo, and Chi joining from the left and right within the territory of Wuhe. Below Gantai and approaching Hongze Lake, the water and land are indistinguishable. In dry seasons, sandbars are everywhere, creating extreme disorder and complexity. From Laozi Mountain along the Hongze Lake levee for over one hundred and forty *li* to Yangzhuang, and then three hundred *li* northeast through Huaiyin, Huaian, Lianshui, and Funing to the sea, lies the old course of the Huai River. Since the Song dynasty, it has been taken over by the Yellow River and is now elevated and rarely flows. This is the overall situation of the Huai River. In total, the Huai River is approximately two thousand one hundred *li* long. In terms of the river course, it is jointly owned by three provinces; in terms of disasters, it is jointly shared by Jiangsu and Anhui. The way to control water is to first understand the composition of the upstream water flow, the actual conditions of the affected areas in each region, and the downstream discharge capacity. An appropriate standard flood level should be pre-determined in the water storage areas in the middle reaches to estimate the urgency of construction and the amount of funds required. According to the Huai River water volume in the most recent twenty years, 1916 and 1921 were years of major floods, with the flood in 1921 being even greater than that in 1916. The measured flow rate was over 14,000 cubic meters per second, and the water level of Hongze Lake was 15 meters above sea level. This is harmful water. If the downstream rivers had the same discharge capacity, the water level would not overflow and inundate the fields, so there would be no disaster. There would be no need to talk about guidance. But in the past, the Huai River and the Yangtze River flowed separately to the sea. Now, there is only the way to the Yangtze River. The full flow rate in 1921 was over 8,000 cubic meters per second, accounting for about three-fifths of the total water flowing into the Huai River. This caused a tragic situation in which tens of counties in northern Jiangsu and Anhui were flooded, with water depths ranging from over ten *chi* to five, six, or seven *chi*. The people of the two provinces regard it as a poisonous snake and a fierce beast, which cannot be kept for a day. This remaining two-fifths of the total water flowing into the Huai River overflows without a destination other than entering the Yangtze River. If this water were stored between Jiangsu and Anhui, the water level of Hongze Lake would already be 15 meters high. The eastern levee of Hongze Lake, which is considered the largest and strongest water control project in our country, is already in a precarious state. How could it withstand further increases? If this water were stored in Gaobao Lake, the water level in ten years would also be more than eight *chi* above sea level, reaching the eastern bank of the Grand Canal, which protects six or seven counties in the lower reaches. If there were any negligence, the people east of the Grand Canal in Gaobao, Xinghua, Dongtai, and Yancheng would suffer the pain of their fish being taken away. Therefore, the problem of guiding the Huai River is the problem of lowering the flood level, which is also the problem of how to handle this remaining two-fifths of the water. Has there ever been a case, in China or abroad, where the water level was lowered but floods still occurred?

I, Qingmu, know that the goal of those who planned to guide the Huai River in the past was to prevent disasters. Is the goal today still the same as before? I dare to say that the disaster of the Huai River is not because it cannot enter the Yangtze River, but because it cannot enter the sea. Even if the water in the Huai River in the most recent twenty years, taking 1921 as the greatest, can be discharged by the Yangtze River, I still dare not be complacent. Because the Huai River is close to the Yangtze River, and the location and climate are completely the same, it is inevitable that the Huai River and the Yangtze River will rise together. Even the water level in September 1921 was sometimes higher than in August 1916, and the discharge into the Yangtze River in 1921 was less than in 1916 because the Yangtze River water level in 1921 was higher than in 1916. Whether my opinion is correct or not, let's not talk about the Huai River water entering the Yangtze River and raising the Yangtze River water level. The sea dikes and weirs in counties north and south of the Yangtze River and the inland discharge are directly affected by the backflow or inundation. Let's not talk about the Yangtze River water rising, even if it is less than a *chi* and the time is only three days. At the moment of slapping against the dikes, this increase, even if it is less than a *chi*, and the inundation, even if it is only three days, is enough to cause a major disaster. For the sake of the safety of the Huai River, there should be another way out as the Yangtze River water gradually rises. Moreover, the water in the Huai River in 1921 was two-fifths greater than in 1916. With today's waterway to the Yangtze River, even without any engineering, the discharge capacity of 9,000 cubic meters per second is its inherent capacity. Now, with full effort focused on entering the Yangtze River, the discharge capacity has not increased. How can we bear to let the remaining water of over 5,000 cubic meters per second cause unprecedented disasters in Jiangsu and Anhui, with the water level of Hongze Lake being 15 meters above sea level? Instead of planning a way out for this water, we set the standard flood level of Hongze Lake at over 16 meters. What is the use of guiding the Huai River? How can we solve the problem of guiding the Huai River to eliminate disasters?

Furthermore, I, Qingmu, have more to say. Matters, whether big or small, each have their principal and subordinate aspects. The safety of the Huai River is the safety of Jiangsu and Anhui. Judging from past facts, focusing solely on the Yangtze River does not address the situation of the Huai River disaster. Even if both the Yangtze River and the sea are considered, the effort may still be insufficient. In the past, the preparations for guiding the Huai River initially focused on diverting the water to the Yangtze River and the sea. After experiencing the major floods of 1916 and 1921, the construction procedure turned to the Yangtze River as subordinate and the sea as primary. Is there any other way? Weighing the advantages and disadvantages, since the harm is great, the primary goal should be to eliminate the harm. The harm of the Huai River is caused by water, and the inundation of fields is caused by the high water level. By lowering the water level, the harm will be eliminated and benefits will arise. If the standard flood level of Hongze Lake is set below 14 meters, ordinary irrigation and transportation will be well served. The design of the main projects, such as the three dams and five ports, should follow the legacy of Jin Wenxiang, returning to the sea via levees. The funds required would be less than 50 million yuan. The construction costs in Anhui would also be similar. Ultimately, it was difficult to raise such a large amount of funds, so it could not be realized. Now, the construction funds obtained from the Boxer Indemnity are only 30 million yuan, which has not yet been allocated. Moreover, whether Jiangsu and Anhui can fully allocate the funds to Jiangsu is uncertain. As for the income proposed by the Engineering Bureau, such as the Yellow River滩地, although nearly one million mu, has been almost released by the Taiwan Camp, official land, and other bureaus over the years. The situation of the lake滩地 is roughly the same. Even if the central and local governments jointly bear the construction costs, it is uncertain whether the 海工程 can be used. If they are divided into two forces, it will inevitably be more short-sighted. This is in terms of funding. In terms of advantages and disadvantages, the effect of returning to the Yangtze River has been described earlier. If 海施工 can be carried out first, then多洩一分入海之水即减少一分地面之災. As for the choice of route, Lin Hongguan River and the old Yellow River were all reviewed once in the past. However, the三壩, such as Gao You以下之車邏新壩南關, also discharged 5,800 cubic meters per second of water during the 1921 flood, but because the坝 water flowed down and overflowed into the fields, the period of启坝 must be after autumn. Such沉災 cannot be easily reduced. If the高寳湖築隄計畫 of the Engineering Bureau can be applied below三壩, or even to涇河 in Bao Ying, then夹隄成渠 can directly reach串塲河 and分輪東川鬥龍新洋射陽等港 to归海上游涨水各坝 timely opening. Even if 江淮并涨 or缩减洩量 for special reasons along the river,归海为之救济. Qingmu deeply hopes to竭全力以助其成,从此江海分流盈虚调剂, and then从从从事于漑灌交通之设计,in in in 得以操纵节制,庶水位得其平,淮灾得其洽,去害生利,江皖永赖矣. 率贡刍蕘,伏祈垂察.谨陈委员长蒋副委员长庄委员王清穆

Zibo

Coal Merchants Thoroughly Explain Their Losses 50

Reply to the Special Party Department of the Jiaoji Railway

Qingdao Correspondence: The Shandong Zibo Zhangwei Coal Industry Association has been on strike since May 21st, and there has been no resolution after ten days. The losses of both the Jiaoji Railway and the coal merchants are significant, not to mention that the society will also suffer the impact. The Special Party Department of the Jiaoji Railway recently sent a telegram to the Association, requesting that the reasons for the losses be announced to all sectors of society so that they can be reported to the central government for verification and instructions, so that this trend can be resolved as soon as possible. The Shandong authorities are also afraid that the strike will be prolonged or involve local security, so they will come out as mediators and try to resolve it. It is heard that the coal merchants said that if the Jiaoji Railway can increase the freight rate and implement it slowly, the coal merchants will resume transportation first, and then wait for the central government to verify and handle it. Yesterday, the coal merchants sent a telegram to the Jiaoji Railway Party Department, explaining the operating conditions and the pain of losses of their colleagues. The text of the telegram is excerpted below: Your telegram said that the market price of coal is always around 24 yuan, and the calculated cost is only 12 yuan. Comparing the principal and interest, the profit is very high. It is necessary to check the value of coal, and there should be a difference between raw coal and lump coal. If referring to raw coal, each ton only needs 3.5 yuan. Lump coal cannot be done for less than 7 yuan per ton. As for small port retail coal, lump coal is the main component. The lump coal of small port coal merchants is mostly bought from the Boshan coal shop, each vehicle (15 tons) is about 180 yuan. The freight from Boshan to Qingdao is 68.7 yuan per vehicle, and the cost of transferring vehicles and unloading labor is about 10 yuan per vehicle. The total of the three items is 258.7 yuan. The loss of stealing and missing tons along the way for each vehicle of coal accounts for about 5%. Furthermore, converting kilograms into pounds, the deficit accounts for about 2%. The total of these two intangible losses is about one ton. Therefore, each vehicle of 15 tons of coal actually only has 14 tons. Moreover, due to the bumps and vibrations along the way, and the results of loading and unloading, 4 tons of coal are turned into pulverized coal. This pulverized coal can only be sold for 12 yuan per ton, which is worth 48 yuan. Subtracting 48 yuan from 258.7 yuan, the remaining 210.7 yuan is the total cost of the remaining 10 tons of lump coal (the division is suitable for 21.07 yuan per ton). When selling, each ton must be added to the small car to send one yuan, so the cost of lump coal must be more than 22 yuan per ton. Other expenses such as interest, factory rent, etc. are not included. Even according to your telegram, the profit can be easily understood if the selling price is 24 yuan per ton. As far as colleagues who operate export mines are concerned, they are even more strong on the outside and dry on the inside. The pain is even more unknown to outsiders. It is found that export coal is generally raw coal. The mountain price of raw coal is about 3.5 yuan per ton, the cost from the mine to Boshan Station is about 2.5 yuan per ton, the donation tax, stone picking, carrying force, and loading force are about 1 yuan per ton, the Jiaoji Railway's special freight is 2.52 yuan per ton, and all expenses at the Dagang Pier are about 1.5 yuan per ton. The loss of stealing and missing tons along the way accounts for about 40 cents per ton. The total cost is as high as 11.4 yuan per ton. Adding land rent, interest, wages, and all expenses, the actual blood cost is more than 11.5 yuan. However, export coal has been ordered according to the contract. According to the contract signed last winter, each ton is unified at less than 11 yuan. Now, although the cost has increased due to various reasons, the pricing cannot be changed due to credibility. We have to bear the burden and deliver the goods. This kind of loss is already unbearable. If the freight rate is increased by 20%, the loss will be even greater, and the merchant is really unable to maintain it. Therefore, it means that the loss of continuing to transport without canceling the price increase is more significant than the loss of closing the door and suspending business. It is also found that the freight rate of any state-owned railway for coal is lighter than that of the Jiaoji Railway. Taking the Jinpu Railway, which is the closest and also in Shandong Province, for Zhongxing, the freight rate per ton per kilometer is only 5 li. From Boshan to Qingdao, it is 345 kilometers. If calculated according to the central government's 5 li, the freight rate per ton only needs 1.725 yuan, which is compared with the Jiaoji Railway's 4.58 yuan (plus 20% is 5.496 yuan) for the mainland and 2.52 yuan (plus 20% should be 3.024 yuan) for export. The difference is not more than doubled. With such a huge difference in freight rates, how can the price of coal in the mainland not increase? How can export coal compete with others? Merchants have repeatedly appealed to request the reduction of the freight rate. Isn't it all moaning without illness? Now, not only has the request for price reduction not been adopted and implemented, but there is also a sudden increase of 20%. Directly, it makes our colleagues unbearable, and indirectly, it increases the burden on the people. What is more unfair than this? Now, I am consulted, and I will report the daily operating conditions of my colleagues and the pain of losses to you. Please check and report to the central government that the price increase should be canceled first and the summer rebate should be restored, and a fair freight rate should be re-established by comparing the freight rates of state-owned railways. On the one hand, please convey to all parties so as to clarify the truth and provide assistance. It is not only the luck of the mine coal merchants, but also the actual benefit of the people of both Shandong provinces. (May 30th)

Liaoning Province

Implementing Governance in the Western Adjacent Mongolian Wilderness 51

Changing the Wilderness Affairs Bureau to a Governance Bureau

The location for governance has also been selected

Shenyang Correspondence: The Western Adjacent Mongolian Wilderness in Liaoning Province has a vast area of fertile land. The Adjacent Wilderness Bureau is set up to survey, measure, govern, and plan for the establishment of governance. The Adjacent Wilderness Bureau previously requested the implementation of governance in the Western Adjacent Wilderness. After deliberation by the Provincial Government Committee, it was decided that the Adjacent Wilderness Bureau would continue to handle it concurrently. The most important thing is to release the Mongolian wilderness to maintain public security. If there is no way to maintain public security, there is no hope for the wilderness affairs to improve. The Wilderness Bureau previously decided to collect 20 yuan of guarding fee for each released side of cultivated land and 10 yuan for raw wilderness, in order to fill the security equipment. It was already expected that this would be the case. As a result, the land could not be released at all. The pre-determined guarding fee was already a pie in the sky. If the land tax was to be collected according to the land, the entire section of the wilderness was said to be 5,6000 sides, but the actual cultivated land was only 2,000 sides. According to the usual practice of the Eastern Adjacent Wilderness, only three of every ten ridges of cultivated land are taxed, and the people still cannot bear the hardship and abandon it to move elsewhere. Therefore, only 400 sides of the 2,000 sides of cultivated land in the Western Adjacent Wilderness actually pay the land tax. A drop in the bucket is of no help. In addition, the people who are in the famine are too busy to save the dead and have no time to care about other things. Therefore, the method of paying land tax according to the land is impossible. It is also found that since the date of surveying and surveying the Western Adjacent Wilderness until now, more than 450,000 yuan of surveying expenses have been spent, more than 200,000 yuan of official wilderness bureau expenses have been spent, and the Mongolian bureau expenses are self-funded and not included. The total expenditure of both official and Mongolian parties is actually no less than 500,000 yuan. It has been released for three months, and according to the report of the Adjacent Wilderness Bureau, only 22,000 yuan of price money has been collected, which is less than 5% of the expenditure. If this continues to be supported and the plan is not changed urgently, the result of the plan to enrich the country and benefit the people will be the opposite. Now the Provincial Government has decided to change the Wilderness Affairs Bureau to a Governance Bureau. The trend of focusing on releasing the wilderness is now changed to focusing on the establishment of governance. The administrative department that was planned to be attached to the Wilderness Affairs Bureau is now changed to the Wilderness Affairs Department attached to the Governance Bureau. This can be effective in adapting to the times. The Governance Plan plans to compile and train a number of police groups in the location of the Governance Bureau and in the wilderness section, according to the method of drawing Ding by household and dividing the area for guerrilla warfare. The guns will be lent from the 1,000 Czech surplus guns purchased and stored by the former Provincial Office, and the price will be paid in installments over the years. The money will not be spent and things will be easily gathered. With the convenience of transportation and the large amount of cultivated land in the wilderness, it will not be difficult for the households to follow suit after the bandits are eliminated in the future. The expenses of the Governance Bureau should be paid by the Provincial Treasury. The detailed plans for how to organize the rest of the Governance Bureau and how to compile, supervise, and be responsible for the safekeeping of the police groups will be made by the Governance Officer. As for the location of the Governance Bureau in the Western Adjacent Wilderness, the Eastern and Western Adjacent Wilderness Bureaus have selected the village of Jiatutu. The soil is fertile, the residences are numerous, the Beidongxin River surrounds it, and the southwest ridges undulate. The mountains and waters are quite good. It is 60 *li* south of the Dalin Station on the Zheng-Tong Railway and 60 *li* east of the Sanlin Station on the Si-Tao Railway. The transportation is convenient. It is 90 *li* north of the Zhaoyou County boundary and about 30 *li* west of the Muchi. The number may not stop there after it is delineated in the future. And the Jiatutu place is actually the center of the Western Adjacent Wilderness and is the most suitable place for establishing a county governance. In terms of the 隣 counties, Liaoyuan is in the southeast and Tongliao is in the southwest, each about 100 *li* away, forming a tripod. It is not only easy to contact, but also convenient to control for developing the Mongolian border and suppressing bandits. In addition, in terms of the surrounding situation, Jiatutu is just located on a straight line with Kailu in Rehe to the west and Changling in Jilin to the east. If railways can be connected in the future, it can become the liaison channel for the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Rehe. The location is very important. It is very valuable to establish a county. The initial plan is to temporarily place the Governance Bureau in the western part of the Sidao Road Sanlin Station Railway near the wilderness in order to manage the Western Adjacent Wilderness and build a new county street at ease to relieve financial strength and help the difficult times. (May 28th)

Liaoning Province

The Movement of Gentlemen and Elders in Fushun County to Move the County Office 52

When Fushun County in Liaoning Province was first established, the county office was originally located in Fushun City. Later, considering the diplomatic relations, the Provincial Office approved the relocation of the county office to Qianjinzai in the fifth year of the Republic of China. However, the Fushun Coal Mine of the Japanese South Manchuria Railway Company is located near the village. Due to mining, the earth's core often shakes, and buildings that are slightly less strong and have been around for a long time often collapse. It is extremely dangerous, and the ground is low-lying. Every summer and autumn, the continuous rain cannot be drained, and floods often occur. It is not a place for the county government to stay. Therefore, in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, the county office was moved to the Datong Inn in the far north of Zhaipu to avoid danger. However, in recent years, due to Japan's encroachment policy, most of the street surface of Qianjinzhaipu has been归于日人, and the rights of the landlords have been almost lost. The Fushun Coal Mine is expanding its mining area, so there is no day in Zhaibei that there is no huge earthquake. The dangerous situation is no less than the place where the county office was established in the fifth year of the Republic of China. The county office is the main brain of a county and cannot always be in a dangerous place. Therefore, the movement to move the county office has started again. However, the gentlemen and elders of the county have different opinions. Some advocate moving back to Fushun City, and some advocate moving to Yulinpu. There is still no consensus. Recently, Zhang Shishi and other gentlemen and elders of the county came to the province to submit a report to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee and the Liaoning Provincial Government, advocating moving back to Fushun County City. From the perspective of national rights, commerce, transportation, and administration, the general idea is that regarding national rights, the most complicated negotiations between Fushun and Japan are related to the Qianjinzai Coal Mine, and the rest are branches and unimportant. However, the county office can handle the negotiation matters in Qianjinzai, and it can also be handled in Fushun City. Moreover, being in Fushun City is better than being in Qianjinzai, away from the encirclement of the concession and having the power of freedom and independence. If it is moved to Yulinpu, it is still in the mining area, and its弊害 is the same as Qianjinzai. It is not a long-term solution. Regarding commerce and transportation, Fushun City has the east-west 瀋海鐵路. It is safe to develop business with ease, and it can臻臻日上, and it can avoid Japanese restraint. The Shenyang Station on the 瀋海路 is more than 20 miles away from Fushun, which is closer than the Fengtian on the South Manchuria Railway to Fushun Station. The transportation of goods should be equal to the 瀋海. Yulinpu is farther away from the station, and the newly opened market is not very prosperous. After all, the transportation is inconvenient. Regarding administration, when the county government was first established in Fushun City, it was inconvenient for farmers to封糧 and pay donations. Now that there is an east-west transverse railway, the 瀋海鐵路 is also planning to build a north-south transportation bridge. The transportation in all directions is convenient and infinite, and the administrative facilities are easy to do and can achieve twice the result with half the effort. Compared to Yulinpu, which is located in a remote corner, it cannot be compared. It is heard that the Provincial Office considers the opinions of the gentlemen to be fair and is now carefully examining them to determine an appropriate solution. A few gentlemen and elders in the province, such as Zhang Shishen, have recently published an opinion letter in addition to visiting the authorities to petition, intending to achieve their goal.

Shantou Implements New Export Tax 53

The Custom House will be abolished from June 1st

Shantou Correspondence: The Ministry of Finance is implementing the裁釐加稅 this year. According to the original plan, the金 will be abolished after the new import tax is implemented, and the常關 will be abolished after the new export tax is implemented. Luo Zongmeng, the Shantou Customs Superintendent, announced on May 23 that the new export tariff will be implemented from June 1st, and the常關 more than 50 li away will be abolished separately. The 常關 in Zhelin, Jinghai, Fukou, Donglu, Huanggang, and Pinghai, which are more than 50 li away, have been abolished this spring.井洲碣石神泉甲子 The 常關 in places such as has been changed to潮海分關, which does not levy import and export duties. Its duties are only to investigate and arrest smuggled goods that evade taxes. The常關 in Shantou (within 50 li) will also be changed to分關 on June 1st to assist潮海大關 in managing内河电船沿海汽船帆船 report tax license放行 and other matters. After the each 常關 is changed and merged, dozens of officials will be dismissed, and the settlement method is still being properly considered.

The Head of the Bandit Gang in Xudong, Who Reigned for Ten Years, Has Been Killed

Xuzhou Correspondence: The bandit gang in Xudong, who appears between Suqian and Sui, is known as the most ferocious one, headed by He Lao Gangzi. The bandit gang has been weakened after successive suppressions by Zhang Huatang's cavalry division and Zhang Zhankui's cavalry third division. He, who has been based in Xudong for ten years, is extremely cunning and has many liaisons with local evil gentry. When the power is strong, he robs and massacres. When the power is weak, he goes into hiding elsewhere and is difficult to capture. On the 20th of this month, He led his gang of more than 40 people to occupy Duanzhuang, a few *li* west of Xin'an Town. Yin, the captain of the engineer battalion of the 12th Division stationed in Xin'an, learned of this and led his team to suppress them. When they approached Duanzhuang, the bandits fired their guns to meet them, and the soldiers immediately advanced and attacked fiercely. At that time, the nearby militia heard the news and rushed to contact Captain Yin to surround Duanzhuang on all sides. On the one hand, they used artillery to bombard and on the other hand, they set fire to burn. More than half of the bandits were killed or injured. The remaining bandits could not support themselves and fled north of the village. They were surrounded and intercepted by the army, and two were captured alive, and the rest were killed. Four handheld machine guns, more than ten shell guns, and more than twenty rifles were seized, and two hostages were rescued. He has been killed in the village. He's real name is Zhengxin, nicknamed Lao Gangzi. The heads of He and the bandit leader Duan Xiaochaung were sent to Suqian from Xin'an Town to be hung up for public display. The army has returned to defense. He, the bandit gang in Xudong, has been rampant for almost ten years and has captured no less than fifty villages and towns. Now it has been annihilated. (28th)

The Ordinary Examination for General Knowledge in Jiangsu Province 54

The Ordinary Examination for General Knowledge in Jiangsu Province was held in the auditorium of the Education Department yesterday. The office arranged everything carefully beforehand, setting up 221 seats according to the number of applicants. The first examination was at 8:00 in the morning yesterday. The chairman of the commission, Chen Hexian, also attended the scene to supervise. There were 151 people in attendance. Yan Chang , the prosecutor of the Zhenjiang Local Court, also attended the scene to supervise the examination. At 11:00, the whole field turned in the papers, and the關防 was solemn and orderly. Wuhu Express News 55

Yesterday, a member of the anti-smuggling unit, surnamed Yuan, traveled from Wuhu on a fast steamer to Wuwei County. A conflict arose with the Wuhu Shipping Association over ticket inspection. After several bouts of fighting, Tong Zhongliang, a ticket inspector for the Shipping Association, Liu Mengru, a liaison officer, and Yuan of the anti-smuggling unit were all seriously injured. Many of the Shipping Association's belongings were also damaged. The Public Security Bureau is now mediating.

The third Wuhu County Administrative Conference was held yesterday at the county government. An opening ceremony was held, and the first preparatory meeting was held in the afternoon, with Yu Yuying and Zhu Di'an elected as chairman and vice-chairman, respectively. The proposals covered the meaning of politics, the conduct of autonomy, the cleaning of finances, the development of education, and the peace and security of the people, among other categories. Various review committees were also selected. The official meeting will continue today, and the conference is scheduled to last two weeks.

The County Chamber of Commerce convened a joint meeting of the chairmen of fifty-four trade associations today to discuss the business tax issue. It was decided to urge the various trade associations to prepare petitions to the tax bureau requesting a postponement of the tax collection. A majority also advocated for a contract system. The second item on the agenda was the reorganization of the merchant corps, and it was decided to increase the monthly donations by 30% while keeping special donations unchanged.

The Anhui provincial examination for certification ended on the 25th. A total of 165 candidates applied for the higher-level exam and 175 for the ordinary-level exam, totaling 340. More than forty candidates from Wuhu went to take the exam. The examination period is scheduled from June 1st to June 8th.

The Wuhu County Consolidation Committee issued two telegrams today: one supporting national peace and unification, and the other supporting the resolutions of the National Assembly. Those who oppose or neglect these resolutions will be regarded as enemies of the people.

The 57th Division of Chen Tiaoyuan's troops stationed in Anqing has been reorganized in the province. The reorganization has now been completed, and more than 300 surplus soldiers were transported to Wuhu today under the leadership of Deputy Officer Wang, from where they will be sent via the Jinpu Railway for demobilization (29th).

The County Party Department convened a tea party at 1:00 PM on the 30th, gathering representatives from various agencies and organizations. It was decided to hold a celebration of the promulgation of the Provisional Constitution and a memorial service for the entombment of the Premier at the Star Cinema at 9:00 AM on June 1st. All sectors will take a day off that day.

Foreign merchants have established offices in Wuhu to purchase eggs, exporting millions of them annually. In the past, the provincial government levied egg duties and educational surcharges. After the abolition of likin, the egg duties were cancelled. Yesterday, the education sector and egg merchants jointly decided to jointly nominate Wang Huanting, a representative of the egg merchants, and Liu Wugang, a representative of the education sector, to jointly collect egg duties from June 1st to contribute to education.

The Anhui Provincial Government recently ordered the Wuhu County Government to immediately investigate all wasteland within the county's borders, categorizing them by sandy wasteland area, soil quality, clay, use, cultivation, forestry, and ownership, with a deadline for submitting a report.

On the anniversary of the May 30th Massacre, in addition to meetings held by various schools in Wuhu City, there were no mass gatherings. Military and police precautions were strengthened on that day, and troops were temporarily stationed to maintain public security (30th).

He confessed to stealing cash and foreign currency from Lianqing Nunnery, as well as clothing from a Mr. [surname] in Dajiaochang, which he pawned and spent. The other thieves involved in the cases are still under strict investigation.

Wei Desheng, a soldier who had previously deserted with weapons, was discovered and captured. Suzhou 57

Business Tax to Be Contracted by Various Industries: The issue of Suzhou's (Wu County) merchants contracting the business tax has not yet been resolved. The province requires Suzhou (Wu County) to contract for 100,000 yuan, but the taxable amount for various industries is still less than 60,000 yuan, a difference of more than 40,000 yuan. The County Chamber of Commerce has scheduled a meeting of the Tax Committee for the afternoon of the 4th to discuss the issue. Director Wang of the Tax Bureau went to the County Chamber of Commerce on the 1st to negotiate, urging the collection to begin as soon as possible in accordance with the provincial order. It is rumored that in the future, various industry guilds will directly contract with the tax bureau.

Request to Postpone Fundraising for Construction Public Bonds: The county government, following orders to raise 200,000 yuan in construction public bonds, convened a meeting of local figures and organized a fundraising committee. Various committee members resigned due to fundraising difficulties. Local figures and organizations held a discussion at the Chamber of Commerce on the 1st, all agreeing that Suzhou Province's public bonds had not yet been cleared, and last year, the public also shouldered construction donations. Furthermore, local construction funds are currently very tight, making it difficult to bear the burden of construction public bonds. It was decided to immediately petition the Provincial Department of Finance to request a temporary postponement of the fundraising.

Verdict in Vinegar Lane Robbery Case: In the case of the robbery at Chai Lianqing's home in Vinegar Lane (Cuku Xiang) inside Feng Gate two years ago, the captured bandits Qian Qiaosheng, Liu Shuming, Liu Shuxian, Zhou Changlin, and three others were sentenced by the local court. Qian Qiaosheng was sentenced to life imprisonment, Liu Shuming and Liu Shuxian were each sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment, and Zhou Changlin and the other three were sentenced to ten and seven years of imprisonment, respectively. The convicts, dissatisfied with the verdict, appealed to the High Court, which yesterday sentenced Qian Qiaosheng to sixteen years of imprisonment and reduced the sentences of Liu Shuming and Liu Shuxian to ten years each. The appeals of the remaining three were rejected.

Wuxi 58

Four Robbery Cases Occur in One Day: Recently, robbery cases in the four townships have been on the rise. Although local police and militia have been strictly suppressing them, few arrests have been made. On the previous day, as many as four robbery cases occurred, which is a cause for concern regarding public security. The details are as follows: (1) The Lao Ban barge from Wuxi to Huashu, Jiangyin, was sailing from the countryside to the city on the night prior. As the boat reached Cuoying Bridge on the east side of Chang'an Bridge, more than ten people wearing tattered military uniforms and civilian clothes, each carrying box cannons and flashlights, suddenly appeared and ordered the boat to stop, falsely claiming to be searching for opium. They boarded the boat and robbed Song Yicheng and a passenger surnamed Lu of a leather bag, a gold ring entrusted to a Mr. Hua for pawning, a gold bracelet, more than twenty yuan in silver, a quilt, a bamboo basket, and several items of clothing. At the same time, the new Huashu barge behind them was also robbed, including a leather robe entrusted to Shen Zhongliang for pawning, more than thirty yuan in silver, and quilts and clothing. The total losses from both boats amounted to about two hundred yuan. The boatmen Zhang Rongquan and Lin Gencquan did not report the incident to the county because it was during the silkworm cocoon season and traffic was heavy. (2) Xia Azheng and his two brothers, farmers from Hualian Bridge near Hongshengli, were slightly wealthy due to their diligence in farming. On the night prior, a small boat from Jiangbei suddenly arrived near the beach, carrying five or six bandits with weapons. After 11:00 PM, they swarmed into Xia's house and robbed them for half an hour before leaving, resulting in a loss of more than one hundred yuan. Azheng's younger brother, Axiang, was also beaten. (3) Shen Jinhua, a merchant from elsewhere, runs a small sundry shop at the south end of Li Bridge, at the border of Kaiyuan and Yangming townships. One morning, someone suddenly entered the shop under the pretext of buying cigarettes. Three bandits rushed in and robbed the shop of all its silver, foreign currency, goods, and clothing. Shen is old and has been completely impoverished by this incident. (4) At Zhou Mingbiao's house, No. 23, next to the Catholic Church at Xiaosanli Bridge outside the North Gate, a large number of bandits also came and robbed them of gold, silver, gold rings, and other items. After Zhou Mingbiao reported the incident, the police from the 5th branch station went to pursue the robbers and arrested the bandits Xu Erbao and Xu Amao on the spot. They were immediately taken to the station, and after a preliminary trial by Branch Chief Peng, they were sent to the General Administration yesterday for transfer to the County Court for strict legal proceedings.

Firearms Seized in Anquan Village, Jiangyin: The Jiangyin-Changzhou Pacification Division Command has been actively conducting anti-banditry operations and has appointed Huang Bingzhong as a detective in the eight counties of Suzhou and Changzhou. Recently, detective Mao Genyuan arrested Han Linbao, a native of Hengtang, Jiangyin, in Shanghai. He claimed that he had been working as a waiter at the Bandai Shengchang Shipping Company in Hangzhou and Huzhou since April of last year. After being sent to the command headquarters, he was interrogated twice. Yesterday (31st), he was sent to the county for custody. On the night of the 31st of last month, detectives from the command searched Anquan Village, Dongwai Sanguan Township, and arrested Lu Jinbao (also known as Lin Cai), seizing five box guns and 350 rounds of ammunition. He was taken to the command headquarters for processing.

They questioned him, and he claimed to be Chen Jinhe, 37 years old, residing in Xuxiang Town, currently serving as an officer in the Southern Five Provinces Water and Land Army and the Presidential Guard. Patrol Officer Kang, believing his words to be incoherent and indicative of madness, ordered the police to search him. Inside his small rattan basket, they found two "Marshal Chen Li" large seals, two small square seals, a "Chen Bi Ji Camp" chop, two wooden Shangfang swords, two tiger-headed Shangfang command arrows, sixty-one red and white business cards, and short shirts, pants, and shoes, all of which were taken to the station. After a preliminary trial by Branch Chief Liu, he was sent to the General Bureau for verification yesterday.

Shen Hancai Stabs and Injures Multiple People: Shen Hancai, a native of Nantong, is 20 years old and has been working at Jiang Songran's rattan shop for the past few years. He then stopped working there and went to work at Wei Jinshun's rattan shop, but was dismissed for being unreasonable. Shen now lives at Tao Jin's house in Sangyuanlang outside the South Gate and teaches Tao's son, Genlin, how to make rattan furniture. Shi Jinhai, who lives nearby, has a daughter named Xiaosanyuan who is quite attractive. Shen Hancai asked Zhang Fubao's wife to act as a matchmaker. The horoscopes have been exchanged, but no ceremonies have been performed yet. Shen often roams around with a flashlight every evening. When the flashlight is shone, the villagers, not knowing what it is, suspect him of being a bandit. As a result, Shen's actions have been noticed by nearby residents. On the evening of the 31st, at 7 or 8 PM, Shen passed by again with a flashlight, and when the light shone, farmers who had just returned from the fields reprimanded him. Shen responded with vicious words, causing a crowd to become angry and beat him severely. Shen struggled to escape home, where he retrieved two small knives and confronted the crowd. As a result, Shi Gensheng's chest was pierced, Shen Yugen was injured in the right chest, Shi Erda was trying to take the knife when four fingers of his right hand were cut off, and Shen Laobing was injured in his left arm and back. At the time, the injured were bleeding profusely. Shen, realizing he had caused a great disaster, fled towards Zifusi. However, the shouts of "catch the thief" reached far and wide. Shi Jinshou and Xia Jintian heard the shouts and gave chase, capturing the perpetrator and reporting it to the Sanliqiao Second Branch Station. The police station sent out police officers, and the four seriously injured were taken to Jishan Hospital in the North Gate for treatment. The perpetrator was taken to the Second Branch Station and transferred to the Public Security Bureau for temporary detention pending interrogation.

Subsequently, a repayment plan was submitted, which was considered appropriate. He then ordered that it be strictly followed. The teachers should consider the difficult times and wait for the administrative authorities to deal with the matter. How can they recklessly threaten to go on strike, wasting the education of children and putting themselves in a dead end? Fire at Niutou, Outside the North Gate: At around 3:00 AM today, the 31st, a fire broke out suddenly on the upper floor of the Tianyuan Silk Shop in Niutou, outside the North Gate of this city, due to carelessness. Educational News

Important News

Ministry of Education's Attitude Towards 67

The Qinghua Expulsion Incident 68

Recognizes Professors' Demands as Inappropriate

Amended School Regulations Cannot Be Revoked

Yesterday, Teachers and Students Held a Meeting and Sent Representatives to Beijing

Nanjing, 1st – The Ministry of Education believes that the Qinghua student unrest, the rejection of Wu Nanxuan, and the faculty's demand to withdraw the amended school regulations are inappropriate. Today, it specifically ordered Jiang Menglin, President of Peking University, to go to Qinghua to convey the Ministry's intentions and declare: (1) The amended school regulations cannot be returned to their previous state. (2) The appointed president cannot be replaced.

Beiping, 1st – Qinghua students held a general meeting today and resolved to form a school affairs maintenance committee to request the local authorities to retrieve the Qinghua seal taken by Wu Nanxuan. They dispatched Lin Wenkui, Liu Hanwen, and Wang Lu to Nanjing within days to petition the Ministry to replace Wu Nanxuan and report the true situation of the unrest. The faculty association also held a general meeting today and appointed representatives to petition the Ministry of Education to remove Wu Nanxuan within days. (Beiping Special Dispatch) Since Wu Nanxuan became president of Qinghua University, it has been over a month, and he has been unable to cooperate with the faculty. Regarding the issue of deans, disputes have arisen over whether deans should be recommended by the faculty and then appointed by the president, or appointed entirely by the president. Recently, after Wu Nanxuan returned to Beiping from Beijing, the Ministry of Education's Directive No. 1683 amended Article 7 of the Qinghua school regulations, "Each of the three colleges of arts, science, and law shall have a dean, who shall be appointed by the president from among the professors," by deleting the phrase "from among the professors." The original Article 10 stated, "Each department shall have several professors, associate professors, and lecturers, who shall be appointed by the president with the consent of the appointment committee, and several teaching assistants, who shall be appointed by the department head after consultation with the president, provost, and dean." This was changed to "Each department shall have several professors, associate professors, lecturers, and teaching assistants, who shall be appointed by the president upon the recommendation of the dean." As a result, most of the faculty believed that this reform was dangerous for the future of Qinghua. On the afternoon of the 28th, they held a faculty meeting and telegraphed the Ministry of Education to replace Wu Nanxuan.

Professors' Document Presented to the Ministry of Education 69

In addition to telegraphing Beijing on the 28th to appoint another wise and capable person, the professors also sent a document to the Ministry of Education. The following is a record of it:

A petition requesting that the school regulations be revised in a comprehensive manner and that another wise and capable person be appointed as the president of the school. This school's regulations were specifically formulated by your ministry with reference to the situation of this school. Since they were promulgated by your ministry in June of the 18th year, they have been followed until now and are very appropriate in all aspects. Even in the past year, when this school experienced unrest and the environment was extremely harsh, school affairs did not come to a standstill, and various plans were able to develop as usual. This was due to the appropriate guidance of your ministry and also to the effectiveness of this school's regulations. The spirit of this school's regulations is to make the president and professors responsible for school affairs to a considerable extent. Therefore, even if the president leaves, school affairs can still not come to a standstill. The University Organization Law promulgated by the National Government on July 26 of the 18th year also gives the highest authority of a university to the school affairs meeting, which is organized by the president, deans, department heads, and representatives elected by the professors. Its spirit and purpose are also the same as this school's regulations. Now, Directive No. 1683 of your ministry amends three articles of this school's regulations. According to the newly amended regulations, the deans may not be appointed from among the professors, and the original appointment committee is also abolished. The appointment and dismissal of professors is decided by the president and deans. Such regulations are not the original spirit of this school's regulations and seem to deviate from the legislative intent of the University Organization Law. The directive from your ministry states that after the organizational and staffing regulations of various universities have been compiled, there will be a comprehensive plan. Therefore, if there are any revisions to this school's regulations, your ministry should consider the situation of this school and make comprehensive revisions. This is the first request of this association. The result of the amendments made by your ministry to this school's regulations is to infinitely expand the power of the president. This occurred at a time when President Wu Nanxuan was reporting to your ministry in the capital. Perhaps your ministry listened to President Wu's one-sided report, which is why there was this one-sided amendment to this school's regulations. Since arriving at the school, President Wu has first caused disputes over the issue of deans. According to the original regulations, the deans of this school were to be appointed by the president from among the professors. Since the promulgation of these regulations, the faculty association and former President Luo had discussed having the faculty association recommend two people from each college, from whom the president would select one for appointment. Within the scope of the law, the opinions of the professors were accommodated. The intention was not to allow the school to be too affected by the president's departure and to allow everything to proceed steadily. Even in the past when there was no president, your ministry telegraphed to elect deans, which went on for a long time and was beneficial without any harm. However, after President Wu arrived at the school, he first proposed to abolish this practice and refused to convene a faculty meeting to discuss the matter, which caused the issue to remain unresolved for a long time. The dean appointed by President Wu from among the professors did not dare to accept the appointment. President Wu happened to be in Beijing at this time, and your ministry amended the regulations. Such is the truth about the so-called deans issue. President Wu has taken over all power in managing the school. Since arriving at the school, in addition to the school affairs meeting not being able to be held due to the unresolved dean issue, the council has not met once. The dean he appointed on his own was unpopular, and when he announced the appointment, the whole school was shocked. Furthermore, because of the dean issue, he convened student tea parties to attack the faculty, using sensational language. There is absolutely no comprehensive plan for the development of academics. Any statements made are fragmented and do not conform to the actual situation of the school. On the one hand, he deceives the faculty, and on the other hand, he treats them like employees. Although the professors want to wholeheartedly assist, they have no way to do so. Before, when the National Government issued clear orders to rectify education, the professors and others were all overjoyed, believing that Qinghua would therefore become more advanced. The National Government also carefully entrusted President Wu with the important task of developing the school. When President Wu first arrived at the school, the professors and others also wanted to jointly contribute to the great cause. However, President Wu has only been at the school for over a month and has already destroyed the good foundation that this school had obtained with great difficulty. This means that President Wu has harmed Qinghua and betrayed the trust of the National Government. The National Government's judgment of people is also something that the professors and others are particularly distressed about after their indignation. We hope that your ministry will consider the difficulty of this school's current situation and specially request that the National Government appoint another wise and capable person as the president of this school. This is the second request of this association. This school has a total of 59 full-time professors. 45 people attended today's meeting. By a large majority of 38 to 2 votes, it was passed to report the true situation of this school to your ministry. We humbly hope that your ministry will take appropriate action. This school will be fortunate, and higher education in China will be fortunate. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Education and concurrently Minister Jiang Guoli of the Qinghua University Faculty Association, May 28, 20th year.

Student General Meeting 70

On the evening of the 28th, the student representative meeting of the school was held and reached a consensus with the professors. At 9:00 a.m. on the 29th, a general meeting of all students was reconvened, with approximately 400 of the 599 students present. The following important matters were resolved: (1) Request the Ministry of Education to dismiss Wu Nanxuan, and have all students march to the principal's residence to request his immediate departure. If Mr. Wu is not at the school, send a letter to Mr. Wu requesting his immediate departure. (Passed by 313 votes) (2) Have all students march to the residences of Chen Shifu, Zhong Luzhai, and Zhu Yicheng to request their immediate departure. (Passed by 295 votes) (3) Request the Ministry of Education to appoint Mr. Zhou Yichun as principal. If the Ministry disregards the public opinion of Qinghua students and appoints another person as principal, the school will resolutely reject them. (Passed by 201 votes) (4) Before the new principal arrives, the association (all students) will send a letter to the faculty council requesting them to temporarily maintain educational affairs, and send a telegram to the Ministry of Education requesting immediate approval. (Passed by 221 votes) (5) Request the library director, Hong Fanwu, to leave the school. (Passed by 199 votes) (6) Request the Ministry of Education to immediately restore the original organizational regulations of the university. (Passed by 213 votes) (7) Send three representatives to Zhou Yichun (who previously served as the principal of Qinghua for five years) to invite him to be the principal of the school. (Passed by 211 votes) After the meeting adjourned, all the students marched to Wu Nanxuan's residence to request his departure, but Mr. Wu had already left. Next, they went to the residences of Chen Shifu and Zhu Yicheng. Mr. Chen came out to meet them, and the student representatives stated the public opinion of the students, requesting his departure. Mr. Chen immediately agreed to leave. All the students cheered three times. They then went to the residence of the newly appointed Dean of the College of Liberal Arts, Zhong Luzhai, to request his departure. This was the situation in the morning. In the afternoon, classes continued as usual.

Local News

Vocational Education Society Vocational Guidance Advisory Meeting 72

The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute of the Chinese Vocational Education Society convened a vocational guidance advisory meeting at 2:00 p.m. on May 30th on the second floor of the society. Attendees included Xu Peihuang, Pan Gongzhan, Hu Chunzao, Ou Yuanhuai, Pan Xulun, He Qingru, Zheng Tonghe, Li Quanshi, Shi Jiuyun, Shen Yizhen, Ni Wenya, Shen Gongjian, Chen Xuanxian, Lu Dianyong, Zheng Siqin, Li Dachao, He Bocheng, Shen Junsheng, Chen Binhe, Huang Renzhi, Xu Xie Kanggao, Shi Heng, Wang Zhixin, Zou Shuwen, Huang Jingwan, and others, totaling more than thirty people. The meeting was presided over by the two directors of the society, Jiang Wenyu and Yang Weiyu, who delivered opening remarks. Following this, Pan Yangyao, Deputy Director of the Vocational Guidance Institute, reported on the recent situation of the institute and the insights and impressions gained after visiting Japan to study vocational guidance. Furthermore, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau, Xu Peihuang, Director of the Shanghai Education Bureau, Hu Chunzao, President of National Tongji University, Zheng Xigu, Principal of Shanghai Middle School, Gao Shiheng of Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, and others delivered opinions. Immediately after that, discussion of the proposed agenda began. 1. The Vocational Guidance Institute proposed that, based on recent experiences in the institute's introduction department, there is an unusual shortage of skilled workers (especially those with intermediate mechanical industrial skills), and asked how to advise various schools to pay attention to training to meet social needs. It was resolved that the Municipal Education Bureau should initiate the organization of a committee to jointly plan and implement practical measures. 2. How to advise various banks, factories, and stores to notify the institute at any time when they need personnel and trainees for selection and introduction, or entrust the institute to conduct examinations on their behalf. It was resolved that, on the one hand, agencies that have already implemented this should be turned into advocacy introductions, and on the other hand, the results and effectiveness of the institute's talent examinations should be reported to the society. 3. Should the institute liaise with the personnel departments of various agencies to promote the implementation of examination and testing methods when hiring talents, in order to ensure appropriate personnel placement? It was resolved that this case can be divided into two stages. In the first stage, the institute will convene a meeting of the heads of personnel departments of various agencies to discuss liaison methods. In the second stage, the testing issue will be considered and implemented by the personnel departments of various agencies. 4. What departments should the vocational specialized supplementary school run by the society establish this year to meet social needs? It was resolved that the subjects offered can be determined by consulting the talent needs of various factories. 5. How to promote the establishment of vocational schools specializing in various industries, each creating suitable talent for their own needs? It was resolved that the educational and vocational sectors should communicate effectively, and that specialized schools should be established within major factories to provide ambitious young people with more opportunities for work-study programs. 6. The society's future direction. It was resolved to liaise more with administrative and industrial agencies to actively promote [vocational education]. If there are any opinions, they can be expressed in writing for the institute's reference.

In total, they won eleven victories in fourteen battles. 41 to 5 Great Victory over Sukmyeong 84

(Huang Jiping, 19th, in Korea)

(Gyeongseong Correspondence) The Liangjiang basketball team competed against the Sukmyeong Women's High School team, the Korean women's basketball championship team, at 5:00 pm on the 18th at the Youth Association basketball hall. The audience was extremely enthusiastic on that day. Our overseas Chinese community accounted for one-third of them. Students from the Renchuan Overseas Chinese Elementary School, more than 100 miles away from Gyeongseong, also came from afar. Counting the Japanese and Koreans, the number should be more than a thousand people. The basketball hall was crowded from top to bottom. Those who arrived late still stood outside the door, waiting quietly for the battle. Li Huize and Jin Zhongwan were invited as referees. When the Sukmyeong players squeezed out from the crowd, each of them was tall and strong, with high spirits. At a glance, they were known to be a strong enemy that was not easy to invade. The Liangjiang players walked quickly into the court, lively and exquisite, and were greatly praised by the Japanese and Korean people. After the two teams fought, there was no progress in passing each other for three minutes. Shao Jinying from Liangjiang won the ball, rushed forward quickly, and shot it in from a distance. Soon, Long Jingyun was fined one point and then Yang Ren passed it over and threw it into the basket. Gao Shun of Sukmyeong was fined twice but missed both times. The first quarter ended with a score of 5 to 0. After a two-minute break, the second quarter began. The Liangjiang players were a hundred times more courageous. The ball was passed to them, and Sukmyeong had no choice. Liangjiang scored fourteen points in a row and Sukmyeong scored two points. The halftime score was 19 to 2. Liangjiang won the applause of the audience. The third quarter started and the Sukmyeong players changed their tactics in the hope of regaining the declining trend. Liangjiang Ren exited and Tu Yunsheng replaced him, making the momentum even stronger. Shao Jinying and Long Jingyun each showed magical calculations and scored twelve points in a row. Since then, the Sukmyeong team was panicked and missed many opportunities. Liangjiang won another 16 to 0. The last quarter was 6 to 3. As a result, Liangjiang won with a score of 41 to 5. Our overseas Chinese compatriots cheered loudly and the whole audience was shocked. The Sukmyeong players burst into tears after a crushing defeat, which is also a fun thing on the court.

Situation Upon Arrival in Shenyang 85

(Shenyang Correspondence) The details of the Liangjiang Women's School basketball team's three consecutive victories in Gyeongseong, Korea, have been seen in the previous correspondence. On the afternoon of the 21st, the players visited the Gyeongseong Science Museum and various scenic spots. On the morning of the 22nd, they went to Pyongyang, which is the second largest city in Korea. There are more than 2,000 overseas Chinese compatriots here. They sent letters and telegrams in advance to welcome the Liangjiang team and held a friendly match with the Pyongyang Women's High School. On the afternoon of the same day, when they arrived at the port at 3:00 pm, representatives from the KMT Direct Branch, the Chinese Chamber of Commerce, and other groups and more than 1,000 overseas Chinese compatriots gave them a warm welcome. They went to Dongshenglou to rest at 5:00 pm and visited Fubilou, Yongmyeong Temple, Xuanwu Gate, Peony Terrace, Miltai, and Jizi Mausoleum. Peony Terrace is the location of the Sino-Japanese War of Jiawu. Because our army was weak in those years, it was unfortunately defeated. Japan annexed our Korean vassals, and their ambition to invade China began here. The peony terrace has a pavilion called the Most Victorious Terrace. The plaques are all written in Japanese to commemorate the Japanese army's victory. The beams of the pavilion and the ancient pine trees around it still have bullet holes. We cannot help but burst into tears when we mourn. At 5:00 pm, we went to the Prefectural Museum to visit, which contains relics from the Lelang Commandery era, the Goguryeo era, and the Jinshi era, all of which are more than 1,700 years old. They are all historically valuable, but it is a pity that they have been lost in foreign lands. At 9:00 pm that evening, all sectors of the overseas Chinese community held a grand welcome meeting. In his speech, team leader Lu Lihua reported on the competition in Japan and Korea and his thoughts after traveling to the east. He also gave sincere words to the overseas Chinese compatriots. On the 23rd, he contacted all parties to arrange the competition. Japanese and Korean schools declined because of insufficient strength, and they went to Andong in the afternoon. On the morning of the 24th, they arrived in Shenyang at 6:30 am. The basketball teams of various schools could not compete because they attended the North China Games. They visited Northeastern University, Beiling, and Fengyong University in the afternoon and left Shenyang for Dalian at 8:30 pm.

Double Victory in Dalian 86

33 to 17 Great Victory over Yayoi

19 to 12 Another Victory over Shinmei

(Dalian Correspondence) The Liangjiang Women's Sports School eastward expedition basketball team left the country on April 25th and crossed the sea to the east. In the previous month and five days, they fought fiercely in various places in Japan for nine times and won six victories. They also won all three battles in Korea. Their name is full of the Eastern Seas and they returned home with honors. On May 25th, they transferred from Shenyang to Dalian and were recruited by the South Manchurian Sports Association to agree to compete with Dalian Yayoi and Shinmei Women's High Schools. Yayoi and Shinmei Schools believed that the Liangjiang team's ball skills were superb, and the long expedition had returned and their experience was richer. This opportunity could be used to receive the effect of "taking the jade of other mountains to attack mistakes." In order to maintain the reputation of the ever-victorious army, Liangjiang had to be cautious in these last two battles in order to achieve satisfactory results. People from all sectors of the Lianbin Chinese community also had this hope. Sure enough, Liangjiang defeated Yayoi in one battle and Shinmei in the second battle. The prestige shook far and wide and it was indeed a well-deserved reputation. In particular, the triumphant sound will remain in Lianbin forever. It is also the most glorious page in the history of women's sports in our country. The two strategic situations are recorded separately as follows:

Liangjiang vs. Yayoi The time was 5:00 pm on May 27th. The heroines of the two teams competed at the Dalian Sports Field. More than 2,000 spectators looked up and danced with joy. Almost all of them were from our Chinese community. Waves of applause were sent into their ears and the warm welcome was evident. After the two teams were set up, they began to fight under the judgment of Harada and Tsukimi. After only two seconds, Yang Ren, the right wing of Liangjiang, got a ball passed from Shao Jinying and shot it in from a close distance to open the record. Suddenly the air became tense and murderous. Kaikyung, the center of the meeting, suddenly passed a ball to Shao and threw it quickly towards the goal. It entered leisurely. Seeing that the situation was not good, Yayoi held an emergency meeting to plan a countermeasure and the entire army fought hard. Akishiyama, the right wing, put in a ball. After several minutes of melee, Zhuang Shuyu and Wang Lan, the rear guards of Liangjiang, guarded the rear, and Yayoi could not succeed. The first quarter ended and Liangjiang took the lead with an advantage of 8 to 3. After a one-minute break, the battle started again. Liangjiang worked hard to suppress the enemy, passed the ball left and right, and Shao and Long frequently put in several balls. Yayoi was at a loss and panicked. At the sound of the gun, the first half ended with a ratio of 19 to 3. Liangjiang won the applause of the audience. The second half began and the situation gradually tightened. Liangjiang's Long passed the ball to Shao and Shao shot remotely, which was actually successful. The two vanguards of Yayoi, Shinsei and Ise, shouted and the entire army tried their best to counterattack and won a lot of balls. Unfortunately, Long, the center of Liangjiang, slipped and his legs were broken. Tu Yunsheng took over and the two sides scored each other. The third quarter was 8 to 9 and Yayoi had one more point, gradually reversing the decline. After the fourth quarter began, both sides worked harder. Shao scored a goal from a distance and Long scored two goals from the center. Yayoi's Ise also showed his skills and scored one point for the penalty and four points. But he was still one point short and the whole game ended. The referee announced the end and Liangjiang won with a score of 33 to 17.

Looking at the strength of both sides, the players of Liangjiang have superb skills, good coordination, and rich experience. This is the main reason for the victory. Yayoi's entire army lacks strength and personal ball skills are also under Liangjiang's. It is natural for them to be defeated miserably. However, their spirit of always being one is also commendable.

Liangjiang vs. Shinmei The Shinmei Women's High School basketball team, the most famous in Dalian, met Liangjiang's ever-victorious army in one game at 5:00 pm on the 28th. The intensity of the battle is self-evident. General fans rushed to enter the venue, which was more crowded than yesterday. This time, the Liangjiang team was the last battle of the expedition. Although some players felt mentally exhausted, in order to maintain the glory of consecutive victories, they fought to the death. Shinmei wanted to respect the reputation of the winning team, so they responded with all their strength. Therefore, the courage of the two teams in engaging in battle cannot be described in writing. The referees, Kuroda and Tajima, had Liangjiang smooth sailing in the first half. The ball often hovered between the three players Shao, Yang and Long. Even if they occasionally lost the opportunity, they still scored more goals. The passing of the Shinmei team was not good. One ball was often not sent out immediately and was taken away by Liangjiang. The first half was 12 to 5 and Shinmei was already dwarfed. In the second half, Shinmei replaced the cadres and agreed on a strategy to proceed in unison, which greatly improved. Zhuang and Wang, the two generals in the rear of Liangjiang, also showed their front and rear coordination skills. One was desperately fighting to the death and the other was skillfully trying their skills. The third and fourth quarters were 4 to 4 and 3 to 3, both tied. As a result, the victory of 19 to 12 eventually belonged to the Liangjiang team. (Reporter's Postscript) This time, the Liangjiang team traveled eastward and the reporter followed the team to investigate the Japanese newspaper industry and all new developments. I deeply feel that all facilities are in good order. The so-called material civilization and scientific omnipotence, Japan is indeed worthy of it. Detailed records will be taught to readers after sorting them out. First, I will briefly describe Japanese sports. It seems that most Japanese citizens understand the true meaning of the word sports. Not only do schools advocate physical education to train students' strong bodies, but also people from all walks of life have a deep understanding of this. Almost all of the time outside of their daily duties is spent on the sports field. All kinds of ball games, track and field competitions, and swimming are available for everyone to practice. The government encourages it and the society advocates it. As a result, there is a universal phenomenon today. Seeing that the bodies of Japanese citizens, regardless of men, women, old and young, are far stronger than those of our country, the future development of their nation cannot be limited. Although the Liangjiang team has won many victories in this eastward expedition, it is only that their ball skills have improved. Comparing the physical strength and perseverance, it is really not enough. I deeply hope that the sports circles in our country will wake up and reflect.
