Local News II

The Truth about Shen Yun's Suicide 155

Confirmed to Be Due to Economic Pressure

Regarding the suicide of Shanghai Art University student Shen Yun, which was reported in yesterday's newspaper, his body has been temporarily placed in the Fujian Guild Hall, financed by his classmates, and a telegram has been sent to his family. The deceased married last year and has parents over sixty years old. His brother's name is Ru Bi, who works for the Ruihe Company in Singapore. Shen Yun's given name is Ru Bao. The claim of Baozhu Yun is false. It is said that the truth about his suicide is entirely due to economic pressure, and the immediate cause was the theft of funds sent from home, leading to financial difficulties and forcing him to resort to this desperate measure. The facts are that two months ago, his brother Ru Bi remitted 80 Singapore dollars, equivalent to about 193.20 Shanghai dollars, from Singapore. However, after the insurance letter arrived at the Art University, it was stolen in transit. Shen Yun has been struggling ever since, borrowing money and pawning items, even pawning his friends' belongings in desperation. On the eighth of last month, he was detained by the French Concession police. He was bailed out by a friend and moved to 165 Rue Dupleix. At this time, he had almost nothing left except for a suit and a few books. Therefore, before committing suicide at the Tiansheng Hotel on Route Macao Bao Lu on the 28th, he sold a suitcase and several books, using the money to buy opium and pay the rent. After Shen's death, several suicide notes were found. One letter to his parents reads: "Dear parents, after this incident, I truly cannot live in this world any longer. Now I have no choice but to take this desperate measure. I believe you will curse me and scold me, but this is what I deserve. However, I hope that you will take good care of yourselves and not grieve or cry for this useless son. I will repay your kindness in the next life. What else can I say? I am determined, truly determined. Unfilial son Bao writes with finality." Another letter was addressed to the principal of Art University, Zhou Qinhao, and another to his classmates and friends. The letter to Zhou stated that the incident was entirely due to economic problems and that old matters need not be mentioned. The letter to his friends stated that the borrowed money could be claimed from Mr. Zhou and that a letter should be written after his death to inform the family of what had happened.

Thugs Shoot Dead the Landlord 156

The Landlady is Also Injured

Ying Lianyuan, a tub maker from Wusong, lived in a bungalow on Pingliang Road, Grand Road. At half past eleven the night before last, he had already gone to sleep when he heard the sound of someone prying open the door. Fearing burglars, he woke up his landlady, Zhao Zhang, and others to open the door to check. They saw three thugs with weapons intruding. Ying shouted "Thieves!" but the thugs had guns and fired nine shots, hitting Ying Lianyuan and Zhao Zhang in vital areas, causing them to fall to the ground immediately. The thugs then fled. Ying's son, waiting for his father to return, went out to look for him and found him lying stiff on the roadside. He touched him and found that he was already dead. He hurried to report to the police station at the intersection of Pingliang Road. By the time the police arrived, the thugs had already fled far away. The deceased Ying Lianyuan was fifty-nine years old and was shot twice, with bullets passing through his chest. Zhao Zhang, a local, was fifty years old and was shot in the right breast and right arm. She is currently being treated in the hospital and her injuries are quite serious.

Huamin Tobacco Company

Lawsuit After Liquidation 157

Da Zhongguo Printing Company Sues for Printing Costs

Judgment for Wu Chengyu to Repay

Wu Chengyu, a Cantonese, was appointed by Huamin Tobacco Company to liquidate the accounts. He published an advertisement on March 25th of the 17th year (1928), convening a joint meeting of creditors and debtors of the company. It was agreed that all outstanding debts would be repaid at 50% and that creditors should collect their dues from Wu's law office before October 15th of that year. Da Zhongguo Printing Company printed decorations for Huamin cigarettes and was owed 4,513 yuan in printing fees. According to the resolution, they were entitled to 2,256.50 yuan. They sent someone to Wu's office to collect the dues. Wu's employee gave them a check with the amount filled in as 1,562 yuan. Because the amount was 694 yuan short of what was owed, they refused to accept it. Da Zhongguo Printing Company then hired lawyer Yang Guoshu to send a letter to Wu Chengyu, questioning the reason for not repaying according to the resolution. Wu initially ignored the letter. Later, he replied that he had already returned the money to Huamin and that they should claim it from Huamin. He then blamed Ling Runxiang and Rong Jieqing, the persons in charge of Huamin's liquidation. Shortly after, Ling died, causing the case to drag on until now. Da Zhongguo, not having received a penny, hired lawyer Yang again to sue Wu Chengyu, Rong Jieqing, and the heirs of the deceased Ling Runxiang for joint repayment. After several hearings in the Special District Local Court, the defendant Wu Chengyu hired lawyer Zhang Deqin to defend him. The court appointed special agents for Rong and Ling. Judge Yang Yi has now ruled that the defendant Wu Chengyu must repay the plaintiff 2,256.50 yuan and bear the costs of litigation. Rong and Ling are not responsible for joint repayment. The reasoning in the judgment is as follows:

"The plaintiff initially sued Ling Runxiang and Rong Jieqing for repayment of the debt. Ling Runxiang stated in court that after Huamin Tobacco Company went bankrupt, Wu Chengyu was responsible for the liquidation. The total debt was over 20,000 yuan. The company's sale price was about 11,000 yuan, which was to be used to repay the debt at 50%. Ling Runxiang and Rong Jieqing sent all the sale money to Wu Chengyu. The plaintiff then added Wu Chengyu as a party to the lawsuit. Adding a defendant due to a change in circumstances after the lawsuit has been filed is permissible by law if it does not significantly hinder the defendant's defense and the conclusion of the lawsuit. Wu Chengyu's defense is unreasonable. Wu Chengyu was appointed as the liquidator by Huamin Tobacco Company, and the company's sale price was sent to Wu Chengyu by Ling Runxiang and Rong Jieqing. Wu Chengyu has not returned the outstanding funds. Ling Runxiang stated this in court. Wu Chengyu claimed that the funds had been claimed by Zhou Yunxun, the company's accountant, because the plaintiff failed to claim the funds on time, and he presented Zhou Yunxun's receipt as evidence. Regardless of whether Zhou Yunxun had the right to claim the funds, Ling Runxiang stated that Zhou Yunxun died in the sinking of the Xinhua ship. Zhou Yunxun has been dead for a long time. Wu Chengyu's claim that Zhou Yunxun received the funds is unprovable. It is beyond doubt that the funds are still with Wu Chengyu. If the funds had been handed over to Zhou Yunxun, Ling Runxiang would have known. The defendant Wu Chengyu, as the liquidator representing Huamin Tobacco Company, cannot ignore the plaintiff's claim. He should be responsible for repayment. Although the defendants Ling Runxiang and Rong Jieqing were employees of the company, the company appointed Wu Chengyu to be responsible for the liquidation, and the defendants Ling Runxiang and Rong Jieqing are not responsible for the liquidation and repayment. The plaintiff's request for a ruling that Ling Runxiang's heirs and Rong Jieqing be jointly responsible for repayment is groundless. Furthermore, the defendant Wu Chengyu did not appear on the date of the oral debate, and the judgment was made unilaterally at the plaintiff's request. Therefore, in accordance with Articles 457 and 98 of the Code of Civil Procedure, the following judgment is made as the main text."

Yongan Second Cotton Mill

Union Bribery Case Concludes with Interrogation 158

Sentencing Scheduled for the Fifth of This Month

The Wusong Wing On No. 2 Cotton Mill union was bribed by the management to cease activities at the end of the eighteenth year of the Republic (1929). Following orders from the Central Party Headquarters, the Control Yuan, and the High Court, the local court thoroughly investigated the matter. After Prosecutor Zhao concluded his investigation and filed a public prosecution, the case was repeatedly reported on in previous issues after court hearings. It has now been learned that the case was concluded at 1 p.m. the day before yesterday by Judge Wu Zhen, along with jurors Qian Chengjun and Zhao Yongzhou, presiding in the third courtroom. Sentencing is scheduled for the fifth of this month. Jin Fan, who was detained, was ordered to be returned to detention to await bail, while the others remained under their original bail. The details of the interrogation are as follows:

Interrogation Records:

(1) Questioning of Shan Han Jian: According to his statement, Tan Huanxiang asked me to lobby. I talked to Tan alone. Later, when the money was handed over, I talked with Yan Gunian and Jin Fan together. The money was provided by the management. Asked who from the management, he replied he couldn’t specifically identify them. Asked who he thought it was, he replied that he observed it might be Guo Shunlin, Ping Ying, etc. Asked where the one thousand yuan was, he replied that the money was given to our union. I know that part of it was used for lawyer fees, two hundred yuan was used to pay off union debts, and the remainder was given to Tan Huanxiang for purposes such as petitions and lawsuits.

(2) Questioning of Yan Gunian: According to his statement, all lobbying matters were decided by the union, which can be verified by the minutes. The reason for asking for money was to obtain evidence for filing charges. Asked if charges couldn't be filed without money, he replied that the union had no funds for filing charges. Asked if Li Yixiong’s accusations against the union were instigated by the management and if the party headquarters was bribed, he replied that he didn't know.

(3) Questioning of Jin Fan: According to his statement, Tan Huanxiang instigated us to resign. We wanted him to have evidence for filing charges, so we resigned. Asked if Hong Dongyi was present when the money was handed over, he replied that he was. Asked where the money came from, he replied that Tan Huanxiang said it was provided by the management. Asked who from the management, he replied that it was ultimately provided by the Wing On manager because he was the person in charge of the factory.

(4) Questioning of Li Yixiong: Asked if he had any feud with Yan Gunian and Jin Fan, he replied no. Asked why he accused them, he replied that the union was not run well. Asked what was not run well, he still replied that it was not run well. Asked if he accused them on his own initiative, he replied yes. Asked who was in charge inside the factory, Li did not answer. Asked if he knew Tan Huanxiang, he said he did not recognize him. He said the workers told me to accuse them, and when asked which workers, he replied that there were some from each department.

(5) Questioning of Deng Yutian: Asked if he had met Li Yixiong, he replied no. Asked why he was asked to submit the petition on his behalf, he replied that he would be given a position after the reorganization. Asked if Guo Shun and Tan Huanxiang knew each other, he replied no. Asked if he recognized Hong Dongyi, he replied no. Asked if Lin Pingying knew them, he replied no. Asked who was in charge inside the factory, he replied that he was in charge. Asked if the one thousand yuan was provided by the management, and if the management was referring to him, he replied that we did not provide the money.

(7) Questioning of Lin Pingying: Asked where the one thousand yuan came from, he replied he didn't know. Asked who was in charge inside the factory, he replied that he was in charge and that he handled the negotiations. Asked if he had been to the party headquarters before it stopped the union's activities, he replied no. Asked if he knew that Li Yixiong was accusing the union, he replied he didn't know. Asked if he recognized Hong Dongyi, he replied no.

(8) Questioning of Guan Fu: When asked whether Yan Gunian and Jin Fan took money within the party headquarters, he replied that he did not know.

Lawyer's Arguments: The arguments then began, and Prosecutor Zhao was invited to attend the court. First, lawyer Xu Shihao argued on behalf of Guo Shun and Lin Pingying, stating that judgment should be based on evidence and not on speculation. Now, Shan Han Jian, Yan Gunian, Jin Fan, and others only stated that Tan Huanxiang and Hong Dongyi delivered a bribe of one thousand yuan. Tan and Hong only stated that the money was provided by the management, but they could not specify who from the management it was. Therefore, it cannot be speculated that Guo and Lin, etc., were the providers of the funds. Wing On is a corporate organization, and all shareholders are the management. Can they all be considered criminals? Therefore, he requested a verdict of not guilty.

Then, lawyer Shen Yong argued on behalf of Jin Fan, Yan Gunian, and Chen Han Jian: (1) (Regarding the facts) The facts are the basis for legal judgment. A slight error can lead to a huge mistake. Therefore, it should be stated first that Yan Gunian is the accuser, not a defendant who has been accused. The outbreak of this case occurred on January 13, 1930, when unemployed workers from Wing On detained Tan Huanxiang, who was selling out the workers, at Ximen and handed him over to the Public Security Bureau. Subsequently, the party headquarters summoned the accusers Yan Gunian and Wang Yuncheng for questioning and detained them. The Public Security Bureau investigated the case and announced it throughout Shanghai. Prior to the outbreak, starting from December 9, 1929, a resolution was passed at a meeting, which proves that Yan, Jin, and Jian, etc., carried out the union's decision to feign cooperation with Tan Huanxiang, Hong Dongyi, etc. On January 11, 1930, all work was completed, and a summary report was submitted to Committee Members Zhu Guilin and Guo Yongxi of the Social Affairs Bureau, and a report was also submitted to the bureau. Subsequently, the workers took the leader to the party headquarters for investigation. Based on this, it can be seen that if Yan Gunian, Jin Fan, etc., had not carried out the union's decision and completed the accusation, this bribery case would still be unknown. Therefore, Yan, etc., are accusers, not defendants. This is clearly evident and is a fact that is very relevant to the law and should be stated. As for the bribe of one thousand yuan, it was used for union purposes and was not owned by Yan, etc. This can be proven by the union's minutes and should also be stated. (2) (Regarding the law) Article 24 of the Criminal Law states that unintentional acts are not punishable. What is considered intentional? The current Criminal Law adopts the "hope" principle, meaning that if a person does not hope to commit a crime but does so, it is not considered intentional. Now, Yan Gunian, Jin Fan, etc., did not hope to obtain a bribe. Evidence shows that they did not possess the bribe, so it is clearly not intentional. Precedent No. 233 from the fifth year of the Supreme Court states that for a crime to be established, knowledge of the criminal facts is required. Therefore, using a forged document requires knowledge that it is forged and intentional use. If it is received and then submitted as evidence in a lawsuit, it cannot be considered using it as a crime. Now, Yan, etc., carried out the union's decision to obtain evidence of bribery and made an accusation. According to the above-mentioned legal precedents, there is no possibility of punishment. (3) (Regarding reason and emotion) The current government advocates integrity throughout the country and strives to eliminate all acts of dishonesty. Both bribery and accepting bribes are secretive acts. If the accuser is equated with the defendant, who will be willing to make accusations in the future? Directly imposing unfair treatment on the accuser indirectly provides considerable protection to the person who bribes or accepts a bribe. How can this be reasonable? Therefore, placing Yan, etc., on the list of defendants is unreasonable in terms of both reason and emotion. Based on the above three points, we should request a verdict of not guilty for Yan Gunian, Jin Fan, and Chen Han Jian, etc., according to the law. As for the facts of Yan, etc.'s accusation, they are all present. We should request your court to punish Yan, etc., according to the law. Yan, etc., spoke publicly and did not have any personal intentions.

Continuing, lawyer Jiang Baolian also argued on behalf of Jin Fan, Yan Gunian, and Chen Han Jian, stating that Li Yixiong's complaint against Jin Fan and Yan Gunian was a matter of management lobbying, which is of utmost importance and should be investigated. Continuing, lawyer Ge Zhaoji argued on behalf of Deng Yutian, stating that Deng Yutian only forwarded a petition for Li Yixiong. If this is considered to be related to the bribery case, then everyone would be in danger of forwarding letters and documents for friends who are unaware of the situation. He requested a verdict of not guilty.

Request for Punishment of Unlawful Chinese Constable 165

Interfering in Civil Matters and Injuring People with a Club

The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association sent a letter to Jones, Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council, yesterday, stating: "We are writing to you regarding a letter from the Shanghai Rice Dealers' Association, stating that our member, Xieren Rice Store, which was previously located at the intersection of North Henan Road and Haining Road, moved to the intersection of Xinzha Road and Changsha Road in February of this year. Therefore, we rented the rooftop to Du Shengchang for continued use. Around 4 p.m. on the 19th of this month, Du Shengchang brought an electricity company bill to our store, claiming that the electricity bill for the rooftop was incorrect and insisted that our Yang Zishan go to the electricity company to verify it. Mr. Yang said that it was late and the electricity company was closed, and that our store was also settling accounts, so he suggested going together tomorrow. Mr. Du refused, used abusive language, and repeatedly hit the counter with his cane. After persuasion from colleagues, he left angrily. Shortly after, Mr. Du sent Constable No. 1666 to arrest Mr. Yang. We believe that the incorrect calculation of the electricity bill is a civil matter and has nothing to do with the police. However, the constable was unreasonable and accused Mr. Yang of disobeying orders, dragging him out of the store. At that time, our employee Zhang Gengsheng stepped forward to dissuade him but was beaten with a wooden club. Then, the constable colluded with Constables Nos. 1714 and 1817, who were patrolling the street, to help the assailant and arrest Mr. Yang and Mr. Zhang, taking them to the police station. Along the way, they were punched and kicked, causing serious injuries to Mr. Yang and Mr. Zhang, as evidenced by the injury certificates from Renji Hospital. The constable, knowing that there was no basis for the charges, falsely accused Mr. Yang and Mr. Zhang of obstructing official duties to vent his anger. The duty of the police is to protect the people, but the constable dared to assault and insult merchants, showing a disregard for the law. The merchants and residents are suffering deeply. We are appealing to your council to seriously negotiate with the police authorities fairly and justly to deter violence. The calculation of the electricity bill is a minor civil matter. The constables intervened and even used clubs to beat people, which is extremely barbarous. After this, the merchants in the concession will live in fear. We are writing to you to request that your council uphold justice and quickly negotiate with the Municipal Council to severely punish the violent constables to punish violence and protect the lives of the people. After verification, we believe that such abuse of power and assault of residents is a violation of the original intention of your council in establishing the police. It seems that appropriate sanctions should be imposed to maintain police discipline. We are writing to you to request that you investigate and handle this matter quickly so as not to fail the trust of the taxpayers."

Two Suicides: One Dead, One in Critical Condition 166

Theft: Chen Shanzhong, a Ningbo native, was riding a tram the day before yesterday when his purse containing fifteen yuan and seven jiao was stolen. Feeling depressed, he had the thought of ending his life. He went to the Renhe Hotel on Sanma Road in the Public Concession, rented a room, and secretly swallowed raw opium in an attempt to commit suicide. Yesterday morning, a tea server at the hotel discovered him and rushed him to Renji Hospital for treatment. He died around 10 a.m. and was sent to the morgue for examination by the court.

Speculation: Zheng Dingji, whose business name is Buqing, was engaged in the gold business. Recently, due to speculation failures and huge losses, he suddenly had the idea of ending his life. He went to the Guangming Hotel on Hualun Mofang Street in the French Concession the day before yesterday, rented Room 31, and secretly swallowed opium paste. He was discovered and sent to Renji Hospital for treatment. It is reported that his life is in critical condition.

Six Axes Due to Jealousy 167

Zhang Dexing, a Shaoxing native, is 35 years old and rents a room above the Tongdexing Fried Noodle Shop at the intersection of Dongbaoxing Road in Zhabei. He previously operated the Yuanda Yong Wine Shop near the vegetable market on Wuzhou Road, but it closed down in October of last year. He is now a land broker. Yesterday evening at 7 p.m., he was invited by his friend Wang Yixiang (a playboy living on Zhaofeng Road) for dinner. Zhang, who is a carpenter, was also present. They all knew each other and enjoyed themselves. After the meal, Zhang and Wang invited Zhang to borrow money from Zhang's father, who lives at Xiyaojiaqiao on Taopeng Road. Unexpectedly, when they were not far from their destination, in a remote and deserted place with no one around, Dexing was walking in front, and Wang and Zhang were behind. Zhang suddenly took out a sharp axe and struck Dexing's head once, his right hand once, his back once, and his right leg three times, breaking his tibia. Zhang ran forward in pain and collapsed in front of a villager's door, shouting for help. The assailant fled into the darkness. Hearing the shouts, the villagers came and reported to the Third Precinct of the Fifth District, which ordered the police to take the injured man to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Zhang was barely breathing and covered in blood when he arrived at the hospital. After an investigation by reporters, the truth seemed to be that it was caused by jealousy.

Plasterer Becomes a Bandit 168

Once Kidnapped Wu Jiaxiang and His Son

Scarred Face Makes Him Easy to Catch

Cheng Guoliang, a Shaoxing native, was originally a plasterer but became a bandit in recent years. On the third day of the twelfth lunar month of last year, he and his accomplices kidnapped Wu Jiaxiang, a wealthy merchant from Cixi, and his son Jinzhang. Later, Wu's wife, Xue, prepared a ransom of 28,000 yuan to redeem them. The Yuyao Public Security Bureau has now arrested a bandit named Zhang in the case, who confessed that Cheng Guoliang had fled to 286 Yuanfang Road in Shanghai. The bureau sent Detective Li, along with Xue, to Shanghai to identify and arrest him because Cheng has a scar on his face, and Xue witnessed the kidnapping and could identify him. Yesterday, Detective Li requested assistance from the Huishan Police Station. The captain dispatched detectives to go to the address and arrest Cheng. He was then taken to the Special District Court. Xue identified the defendant in court as the kidnapper, but Cheng denied it. Judge Feng stated that the requesting personnel did not bring formal documents requesting extradition, so the procedures were incomplete. He ordered that the bandit be detained temporarily and that the Zhejiang Provincial Government be prepared to send someone to Shanghai to extradite him for interrogation.

Thunderstorm Yesterday 169

Ended in Half an Hour

At 11:20 a.m. yesterday, there was a sudden rumble of thunder in Shanghai, and dark clouds gathered. In an instant, it began to rain. The rain stopped, and the thunder subsided in about half an hour, and the sun reappeared.

Motorist Who Killed a Pedestrian 170

Sentenced to Four Months in Prison

Lu Quanfu, a motorist from Chongming, was driving car No. 15848 around 6 a.m. on the 21st of last month when he was speeding near Ningwu Road on Yangshupu Road. He knocked down and injured Ma Dianfu, a Jiangbei worker from the Dakang Cotton Mill, who was walking on the road, and he died. He also injured Hu Yezi and Cao Taosheng from Yancheng. After an investigation, the constables arrested Lu. The deceased was reported to the authorities, and after an examination, the coroner ordered that the deceased's wife, Gao, be provided with a coffin. The injured were sent to the hospital for treatment and have now recovered. The police station summoned witnesses the day before yesterday and sent Lu Quanfu to the Special District Court. Judge Feng interrogated him. The deceased's wife, Gao, stated that her husband earned 20 yuan a month working and was now killed, leaving behind two children. She requested that the defendant compensate for funeral expenses of 300 yuan and provide 3,000 yuan in compensation. Hu and Cao also described the circumstances of the defendant's accident. Chen Quanfu confessed that his wife and children had arrived from his hometown on the day in question, and he had secretly driven his employer's car to the wharf to pick them up. On the way, a child suddenly crossed the road, and he swerved to avoid the child, unfortunately causing the accident. Judge Feng sentenced Lu to four months in prison. The family of the deceased was told to file a separate lawsuit in the civil court to seek compensation.

Brother-in-Law Gathers Crowd to Rob Sister-in-Law 171

Threats and Rape in Hotel

Sent to Court for Severe Punishment According to Law

Xu Genshan, a local resident of Xujiazhai, North of the Flying Machine Ground on Sheshan Road in West Shanghai, is a Taoist priest. He only has two daughters, the elder named A'di and the younger named Linbao. Xu Genshan feared that his lineage would end, so in the fourteenth year of the Republic (1925), he hired Shen Shichang from Wang Manshui Bridge to be his son-in-law, renaming him Xu Yongsheng. In the winter of the eighteenth year of the Republic (1929), he officially married A'di. A'di died in childbirth last autumn (August), and the child also died shortly after. However, Yongsheng does not engage in honest work and has become a scoundrel. Last month, he was driven out by his father-in-law, Xu Genshan. Suddenly, on the evening of the day before yesterday (May 31) around 8 p.m., Yongsheng gathered six or seven people and, taking advantage of his parents-in-law not being home, suddenly robbed his sister-in-law Linbao. They put her in a car and drove quickly east to Room 14 of the Huimin Hotel on Sisede Long Road in the French Concession of Xujiahui. They threatened and raped her, but Linbao vowed to die resisting, so her clothes were torn. She shouted at the top of her lungs. At that critical moment, Detective Ding Wensheng from the French police station was patrolling and entered the room. He brought the man and woman back to the police station for questioning. The captain interrogated them and, because the case occurred in the interior, sent them to the Second Precinct of the Sixth District of Xujiahui yesterday afternoon. After a preliminary hearing by Chief Liu, the woman Xu Linbao, who is 21 years old and unmarried, stated that she was suddenly robbed by her brother-in-law Xu Yongsheng, who had gathered a crowd, and taken to the Huimin Hotel in Yangjiaku, where she was threatened and raped. The woman resisted and shouted for help, but she was unable to resist and was eventually raped for thirty minutes. Later, the detective arrived and took them back to the police station. Xu Yongsheng (Shen Shichang) stated that he is 24 years old and a Taoist priest. He married into the Xu family when he was 18 years old. Now, because his wife and children have died, and he has recently been driven out by his father-in-law, he invited people to rob his sister-in-law to be his wife, but he did not rape her. Chief Liu stated that the case involved gathering a crowd to rob and threatening rape, which is extremely illegal. He ordered them to be detained and sent to the local court this morning to be prosecuted according to the law.

Pitiful Children 172

Ji Lianxin: Ji Yunxin, a 15-year-old girl from Guangdong, was trafficked to Shanghai after her parents died. Two years ago, she was sold to the Liu family in Dongma Bridge as a maidservant. She was abused by her master and could not bear the suffering. At 12 p.m. the day before yesterday, she escaped to the Hubei Noodle Shop opened by Cheng Xinzhen at 150 Dajing Road and ate noodles. She stayed until the noodle shop closed and still did not return. Cheng asked her why she was unwilling to go home. She said that she could not bear the abuse of her master and pleaded for help. Cheng let her stay for one night. At 1:05 p.m. yesterday, he called the patrolman Wang Yuqi to take Ji Lianxin to the Second Precinct of the Second District. After questioning by Chief Xu, he learned the truth of the matter and felt sorry for her. Furthermore, the law does not allow keeping maidservants, which is a violation. She was sent to the Third Department for Relief.

Zhu Dalou: Song Dalou, a 12-year-old boy from Tianjin, lives in Tianjin. He was buying things outside and returned home a little late, so his parents kicked him out. Thinking that he had acquaintances in Shanghai, he snuck onto a ship to Shanghai. However, after arriving in Shanghai, he did not know the way and did not know where his acquaintances lived. He wandered around the Jinjia Arch in the city crying. Patrolman Fan Zerun from Post 32 took him to the First Precinct of the Second District. After questioning by Chief Xu, he sent him to the Third Department for Relief of the General Bureau.

Children's Health Competition 173

Conclusion of the Health Campaign of the Young Women's Christian Association

The Shanghai Young Women's Christian Association, in order to promote health, selected eighteen children who were examined during the health campaign and found to be healthy and free of disease. A health competition will be held at the association's premises on Nanjing Road at 3 p.m. today (June 2). Doctors Xu Naili, Ni Fengsheng, and Chen Hongda have been invited to re-examine and judge them. The ten healthiest children will be divided into two groups, A and B, with five members each. The association's medals and milk powder from various milk powder companies, as well as Quaker oatmeal and oatmeal cookies, will be awarded as encouragement. Tea and refreshments will also be provided, creating a lively event.

Hwadar Pharmacy Invents No. 2 Bottle of Chicken Essence 174

Now is the summer season, and the weather is unpredictable. People often feel tired and sleepy and are prone to headaches and chest tightness. The Lion Brand Beef Essence and Chicken Essence from Marta Pharmacy, managed by the German Hwadar Pharmacy, can invigorate the spirit and prevent diseases. It is the only guarantee for our health during unpredictable weather. Therefore, the pharmacy's business has been particularly prosperous recently. In order to promote and popularize it, the pharmacy has newly invented the No. 2 bottle of chicken essence, priced affordably so that even common people with insufficient purchasing power can afford to buy it, which is a great benefit to society.

Wireless Radio Film Lecture 175

In recent years, sound films have been extremely popular with audiences due to their novelty. However, at the same time, some audiences have strongly opposed the sound in these films, saying that they have no artistic value. Yesterday, the broadcasting station of the Guohua Electrical Appliance Store in Shanghai, in response to audience requests, invited film writer Zhou Shidong to give a lecture on the matter. The topic of the lecture was "Sound Films and Audiences," in which he said that sound films will have no place in the future.

克倫 Hospital Cures Critical Illness 176

The 克倫 (Ke Lun) Hospital on Xizang Road, founded by the renowned venereal disease specialist Zhang Kelun (張克倫) for over a decade, has been known for its effectiveness in treating various ailments, with every medicine bringing about a cure. Recently, a certain gentleman in the financial world suddenly suffered from red, swollen eyes with a copious flow of pus. Despite seeking treatment from various doctors, none proved effective, and the condition worsened to the point of near blindness. An ophthalmologist determined that the illness originated from leukorrhea and referred him to 克倫 Hospital for treatment. After examination by Dr. Zhang, it was diagnosed as gonorrheal ophthalmia. Using the latest scientific methods, Dr. Zhang treated him several times, resulting in a complete recovery. Deeply grateful, the gentleman intends to commend Dr. Zhang for his exceptional medical skills. This further demonstrates Dr. Zhang's profound medical expertise.

The 惠羅 (Hui Luo) Company, located at the corner of Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road, received a telegram from its head office yesterday, ordering an immediate special clearance sale. Gong Hansheng Practices Medicine to Benefit the World 178

Mr. Gong Hansheng (龔漢聲) of Nanhui is the intelligent son of the renowned physician Gong Kaifu (龔愷甫). After reaching adulthood, he began assisting his father in medical practice. Later, he came to Shanghai to work as a journalist for the 新浦東報 (Xin Pudong Bao) newspaper while simultaneously studying diligently with the renowned physician Xu Xiangren (徐相任). Xu had obtained the true teachings of Fei Shengfu (費繩甫) of the Menghe school of medicine, and Mr. Gong also possessed a thorough understanding of this tradition. Having now completed his apprenticeship, he has established a clinic at No. 89 Jiang Lane, 3rd Ma Road (opposite 新惠中 Xin Hui Zhong), where he will use his knowledge to benefit and save people.

Palm Olive Company Sues Central Soap Factory 179

The Shanghai Palm Olive Company, located at No. 3 Guangdong Road, sells two types of scented soap: Palm Olive and Vioris. The company has discovered that the Coconut and Violet soaps sold by the Central Soap Factory at No. 218 Yuezhou Road have trademarks that bear a suspicious resemblance to theirs, suggesting imitation. Consequently, they filed a lawsuit with the Special District Court. Yesterday, Judge Xiao Xiefen (蕭燮棻) summoned the parties for questioning. Attorneys Ah Leman (阿樂滿) and Bao Ren (包仁), representing the plaintiff, argued that the defendant's soap sales involved plagiarism of the Palm Olive Company's soap. Weng Rongbing (翁榮炳), the manager of the defendant Central Soap Factory, also testified, explaining the process of marketing his soap. After reviewing the testimonies, Judge Xiao adjourned the hearing to June 10.

News from Various Labor Unions 180

Fourth District Silk Reeling Industry Labor Union: The 12th meeting of the executive and supervisory committees was held yesterday, chaired by Chen Xiupu (陳秀普). (1) It was recently discovered that a small number of factory owners are using layoffs as a pretext to coerce workers into signing harsh conditions. The question arose as to how to deal with this. The resolution was: (A) Submit the matter to a joint meeting of the city's silk reeling industry unions for discussion. (B) The union will first notify all members to firmly reject such demands and secretly report any incidents to the union for investigation. (2) The Social Bureau is currently conducting unemployment registration for union members. A decision was needed on whether to notify unemployed members to report to the union first and then register with the Social Bureau. The resolution was passed. (3) The positions of director Pan Jiping (潘季平) and supervisor Xu Huisheng (徐惠生) have become vacant due to their resignations. A decision was needed on how to fill these vacancies. The resolution was that, according to law, Fei Fengtai (費鳳臺) should fill the director position, and Yang Xinmin (楊新民) should fill the supervisor position. The secretariat was instructed to notify them accordingly. (4) A decision was needed on whether to retain standing supervisor Chen Xinglin (陳杏林) for work and provide a living allowance. The resolution was that Chen Xinglin should be retained for work with a temporary living allowance of $14. (5) A decision was needed on whether to visit factories to inquire about workers' living conditions and accurately fill out the reports. The resolution was that the organization department should handle it. Meeting adjourned.

Pharmaceutical Workers Mutual Benefit Society: The fourth executive committee meeting was held the day before yesterday, chaired by Zhao Zhenhui (趙振輝), who opened the meeting with customary formalities. (1) The society's recruitment of members has concluded. According to the review, 198 applicants were qualified, 22 were unqualified, and 5 were still under investigation pending a decision after investigation. There was also one applicant who needed to reapply after obtaining a union certificate because the certificate was inconsistent. A vote was requested on whether these steps were appropriate. The meeting resolved to approve all the above steps. (2) A decision was needed on whether to extend the deadline for issuing society membership certificates to newly recruited members. The meeting resolved to extend the deadline to June 6 for ten days. If a member had to return home due to circumstances, an extension would be granted, and the distribution would be scheduled over three days with a notice to all members. (3) A decision was needed on whether to designate committee members to be responsible for issuing membership certificates. The meeting resolved that it was necessary to designate committee members. Chen Hesan (陳荷三) and Li Jinsheng (李金生) were designated for the first district on June 6, Ru Shensxiu (茹愼修) and Tang Wenliang (唐文亮) on the 7th, Lin Jinfu (林錦福) and Shi Zongliang (史宗良) on the 8th, Ye Baozhong (葉寳忠) and Wang Kaichun (王開春) on the 9th, and Hu Ruirong (胡瑞榮) and Zhang Tongfu (張通夫) on the 10th. They would work with Zhao Zhenhui (趙振輝) and Fang Qingjian (方清鑑) to handle the process. (4) The society's investigation of membership transportation expenses amounted to $40 or $50. The union's finances were tight and could not cover the costs. A decision was needed on how to proceed. The meeting resolved to wait until the union's May dues were collected before making a decision or borrowing the funds from the society. (5) The society collected a $2 membership fee and monthly dues up to May, with the June dues going to the union. A vote was requested on whether these steps were appropriate. The meeting resolved to proceed accordingly. (6) A letter from manager Yu Liangxin (郁良心) and Shi Qintang (施琴堂) requested permission for a friend to join the society. A decision was needed on how to proceed. The meeting resolved to reply to Shi Qintang that the deadline had passed and accommodation was not possible. (7) A decision was needed on how to handle workers from Cai Tongde (蔡同德) who had not joined the union. The meeting resolved to hand it over to the union's executive and supervisory committees for handling.

Laundry Workers Professional Union: The second preparatory committee meeting was held the day before yesterday, chaired by Chen Yuqing (陳宇清). (A) Report matters briefly. (B) Discussion matters (1) Adopt the draft constitution of the union. The resolution was to revise and adopt it, then submit it to the Municipal Training Committee for approval. (2) Zhang Dingxing (張鼎興) submitted a request for subsidies from the Municipal Training Committee due to the union's financial difficulties. The resolution was passed. Items three, four, and five were omitted.

Weather Report 181

Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: Cloudy with rain along the coast, clear with fog in the Yangtze River basin. Northeast to southeast winds in the Yellow Sea and East China Sea. No weather reports from Taiwan. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 79°F and the lowest was 61.2°F. On the same day last year, the highest was 87.3°F and the lowest was 71.2°F.

Letter to the Editor 182

To the esteemed editors, Upon reading your newspaper, I saw a news item titled "Lin Lin Suddenly Arrested," which stated that Lin Lin was a student at the 文生 (Wen Sheng) English School. After investigation, our school has no student by the name of Lin Lin. To prevent any misunderstanding from the outside world, I am writing to request a correction and ask that this letter be published in the "Letters to the Editor" column. Sincerely, 文生 Higher English School, June 1st.

Shanghai Market

Market News 183

Huada Pharmacy on Avenue Foch (福煦路華達藥行) announces that the manager of this store, the German Martha Pharmaceutical Factory, has a potent brand of chicken broth, 獅力牌 (Lion Strength Brand), that comes in large bottles, with a price slightly above the reach of the average person, making it difficult to purchase at any time. Knowing that it has great benefits but lacking the purchasing power is a shame. Recently, to remedy this deficiency, the factory has specially produced a No. 2 bottle, which sells for only two dollars, to make it more accessible. Lately, the purchase of No. 2 chicken broth has been very enthusiastic, indicating that this special production is quite suitable for our society's needs.

Meida Silk and Foreign Goods Company on 4th Ma Road (四馬路美大綢緞洋貨公司) announces that our company has always been known for its low prices and good quality. Recently, as summer is approaching, it is the season for all walks of life to make summer clothes. Therefore, starting from the previous day, we are holding a summer grand sale and establishing a stock clearance sale section and a remnant fabric section. For any clothing material purchased, only one dime is charged per piece, etc.

Since its founding, the Old Duck Brand (老鴨牌) cross-stitch embroidery thread has enjoyed a widespread reputation. According to Mr. Xue Zuyin (薛祖蔭) of the sales department, the raw materials are entirely domestic, and the surface and quality are no different from imported products, with prices kept as low as possible. As a result, sales are strong both in the north and south. We are currently adding workers to increase production. Those who patronize us are requested to visit the Yifenghao (義豐號) store in Chunyuan Lane (春源里), West Old Warehouse Street (西舊倉街), Old North Gate (老北門), where we will directly discuss the matter.

Theater News 184

The 百星 (Bai Xing) Grand Theater at the intersection of Route des Soeurs (老靶子路) and Avenue Haig (福生路) announces that starting yesterday, we are screening the latest production of the 聯華 (Lianhua) Company, the unprecedentedly magnificent epic "The Conflict of Love and Desire" (愛慾之爭). This film is produced by Luo Mingyou (羅明佑) and stars Wang Cilong (王次龍), Zhou Wenzhu (周文珠), Tang Tianxiu (湯天繡), and other stars. It depicts the subtleties of love and the mystery of the conflict between the spirit and the desires, making it the crown jewel of domestic films.

The 大東 (Da Dong) Film Company announces that despite the recent rainy weather, we have not relaxed our efforts in film production. Yesterday, we filmed the farewell scene from the second episode of "The Chivalrous Hero's Biography" (俠義英雄傳). Director Wang Fuqing (汪福慶) and male and female stars Zhang Qingtao (張清濤) and Zhang Jingzhen (張靜珍) played the lead roles, and their performances were excellent in every way, with the delicacy of their movements being unparalleled in domestic films.

The 華東 (Hua Dong) Film Company announces that the historical epic "Huanghuagang" (黄花崗), which has been in preparation for a long time, is now ready and will begin location shooting on June 1. Manager Song Tingbin (宋廷濱), director Yang Zuixia (楊醉俠), assistant director Dong Qiman (董綺蔓), lead director Ma Liqiaoershi (馬麗喬爾士), and lead actor Shi Daxing (士大星) are all involved. It is rumored that the plot is mysterious and the background is magnificent. When the film is completed and released, it will surely be spectacular.

The 華劇 (Hua Ju) Film Company announces that since the release of the first two episodes of "King of Ten Thousand Heroes" (萬俠之王), everyone has been rushing to see them, and it has been a resounding success. Now, the third episode of "King of Ten Thousand Heroes" is directed by martial arts star Zhang Huimin (張惠民) and is even more thrilling and suspenseful. The oddity of the locations, the precariousness of the terrain, and the depth of the performance are unparalleled in domestic martial arts films. The interior scenes are also quite grand and magnificent. In addition, Miss Wu Suxin's (吳素馨) performance as Ru Gu (茹姑), a delicate and weak woman who is able to fight enemies and move like the wind on the rugged, protruding, and winding mountain crags, is admirable. The performances of Misses Wu Susu (吳素素) and Zhang Jianying (張劍英) are lively, strange, precise, and unconventional, showing true artistic talent. Therefore, the success of this film is not easy. The plot of this film is bizarre, and the intention is profound, making it worthy of appreciation by martial arts experts, worthy of study by explorers, worthy of material by writers, and worthy of depiction by artists. The editing is now complete, and it is scheduled to be released on June 5 at the Central Theater.
